NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
Form No. 155
[See rule 329]
Companies Act, 1956
[Members voluntary winding-up]
In matters of VIBGYOR GRAPHICS AND RESEARCH CENTRE LIMITED
Notice Convening Final Meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the members of the above-named
company will be held at Registered Office of the Company situated at No. 50, E.V.K. Sampath Salai, Vepery, Chennai600 007, on Friday the 27th day of June, 2014 at 10.00 A.M. for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing
the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any
explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner
in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Dated this 15th day of May 2014 at Chennai.
Chennai-600 007,
29th May 2014.

R. PARANJOTHI,
Liquidator.

NIPPON PAINT & SURFACE CHEMICALS PRIVATE LIMITED
Registered Office: Plot No. K-8(1), Phase-II, Sipcot Industrial Park, Mambakkam Village, Sriperumbudur-602 105
CIN: U24222TN2004PTC095373
Notice is hereby given under Section, 485(1) of the Companies Act, 1956 that the members of the company in the
Extra-ordinary General Meeting held on 24-5-2014 have passed the following resolution as a special resolution.
“ RESOLVED THAT Pursuant to Section. 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the consent of the members be and
is hereby accorded to wind up the company voluntarily.”
Chennai,
30th May 2014.

KANG WOEI SHIN,
Director.

P. Harikumar, aged 18 Years, male, who is mentally retarded, son of K. Padmanaban and V. Uma Maheswari, born
on 7th May 1995, residing at No. 6/69, First Floor, Ganapathi Street, West Mambalam, Chennai-600 033, Shall henceforth
be known as P. SARAVANAN.
Chennai,
30th May 2014.

V. UMA MAHESWARI,
